# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyAuditLogger for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyAuditLogger` in `pkg/policy/` that provides structured logging of policy
evaluation decisions for audit and debugging purposes.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** with:
   - `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with configurable log level and output
   - `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` method
   - `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` method
   - Integration with Cilium's existing logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
   - Support for JSON-structured audit log output

2. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `logfields` package for structured log fields
   - Follow the `SelectorCache` interaction pattern
   - Use `lock.Mutex` from `pkg/lock/` for thread safety

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/distillery.go` — policy decision evaluation
- `pkg/policy/selectorcache.go` — SelectorCache for identity matching
- `pkg/policy/types.go` — policy types and interfaces
- `pkg/logging/logfields/logfields.go` — structured log field constants
- `pkg/lock/lock.go` — Cilium's lock primitives

## Success Criteria
- PolicyAuditLogger struct and methods exist
- Uses Cilium's logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
- Has LogDecision method with policy verdict logging
- Thread-safe implementation
- Test file exists with test functions

type SelectorCache struct {
	mutex lock.RWMutex

	// idCache contains all known identities as informed by the
	// kv-store and the local identity facility via our
	// UpdateIdentities() function.
	idCache scIdentityCache

	// map key is the string representation of the selector being cached.
	selectors map[string]*identitySelector

	localIdentityNotifier identityNotifier

	// userCond is a condition variable for receiving signals
	// about addition of new elements in userNotes
	userCond *sync.Cond
	// userMutex protects userNotes and is linked to userCond
	userMutex lock.Mutex
	// userNotes holds a FIFO list of user notifications to be made
	userNotes []userNotification

Excellent! I've successfully implemented the `PolicyAuditLogger` for Cilium. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Implementation Summary

### Files Created

1. **`pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** (122 lines)
   - `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with configurable log level and output
   - Thread-safe implementation using `lock.Mutex` from Cilium's lock package
   - Integration with Cilium's logrus-based logging framework
   - Structured logging with `logfields` package constants

2. **`pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go`** (259 lines)
   - 11 comprehensive test functions covering all functionality
   - Tests for logger creation, decision logging, evaluation logging
   - Thread safety verification with concurrent access tests
   - JSON audit log output testing

### Key Features

✅ **PolicyAuditLogger Struct**
- Embedded `lock.Mutex` for thread safety
- `logLevel` field for configuration
- `log *logrus.Entry` field for structured logging

✅ **Core Methods**
- `NewPolicyAuditLogger(level)` - Creates a new logger with specified log level
- `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` - Logs policy decisions with structured fields
- `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` - Logs policy evaluation results
- `SetLogLevel(level)` - Updates the log level configuration
- `GetLogLevel()` - Retrieves the current log level
- `LogAuditJSON(auditData)` - Logs audit data as JSON for programmatic parsing

✅ **Cilium Pattern Compliance**
- Uses `logging.DefaultLogger` with LogSubsys field for subsystem identification
- Integrates with `logfields` package for standard field names
- Follows `SelectorCache` interaction pattern with proper RWMutex locking
- Thread-safe implementation using `defer pal.Unlock()` pattern
- Uses `logrus.Fields` for structured, key-value logging

✅ **

identity: The numeric identity of the subject\n// - policy: A string identifier for the policy being evaluated\n// - verdict: The decision result (e.g., \"allow\", \"deny\")\n// - reason: A string explaining the decision\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n// - ctx: Context for the operation\n// - policyKey: The policy types.Key being evaluated\n// - selectorCache: The SelectorCache used for identity matching\n// - result: A boolean indicating if the policy evaluation allowed or denied\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey types.Key, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tresultStr := \"deny\"\n\tif result {\n\t\tresultStr = \"allow\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Create structured log entry with audit information\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"policyKey\":      policyKey.String(),\n\t\t\"evaluationResult\": resultStr,\n\t}\n\n\t// Include selector cache information if available\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\t// Add cache size information for audit trail\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RLock()\n\t\tcacheSize := len(selectorCache.idCache)\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tfields[\"selectorCacheSize\"] = cacheSize\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(fields).Info(\"Policy evaluation\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.log = auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level of the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n\n// LogAuditJSON logs structured audit information as JSON for programmatic parsing.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogAuditJSON(auditData map[string]interface{}) error {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Convert to JSON string for logging\n\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(auditData)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpal.log.WithError(err).Error(\"Failed to marshal audit data to JSON\")\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithField(\"audit_json\", string(jsonData)).Info(\"Audit event\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n",

  "content": "// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n\npackage policy\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types\"\n)\n\nvar auditLog = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, \"policy-audit\")\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n\tlog      *logrus.Entry\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t\tlog:      auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level),\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with structured fields.\n//\n// Parameters:\n// - identity: The numeric identity of the subject\n// - policy: A string identifier for the policy being evaluated\n// - verdict: The decision result (e.g., \"allow\", \"deny\")\n// - reason: A string explaining the decision\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n// - ctx: Context for the operation\n// - policyKey: The policy types.Key being evaluated\n// - selectorCache: The SelectorCache used for identity matching\n// - result: A boolean indicating if the policy evaluation allowed or denied\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey types.Key, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tresultStr := \"deny\"\n\tif result {\n\t\tresultStr = \"allow\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Create structured log entry with audit information\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"policyKey\":      policyKey.String(),\n\t\t\"evaluationResult\": resultStr,\n\t}\n\n\t// Include selector cache information if available\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\t// Add cache size information for audit trail\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RLock()\n\t\tcacheSize := len(selectorCache.idCache)\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tfields[\"selectorCacheSize\"] = cacheSize\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(fields).Info(\"Policy evaluation\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.log = auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level of the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n\n// LogAuditJSON logs structured audit information as JSON for programmatic parsing.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogAuditJSON(auditData map[string]interface{}) error {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Convert to JSON string for logging\n\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(auditData)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpal.log.WithError(err).Error(\"Failed to marshal audit data to JSON\")\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithField(\"audit_json\", string(jsonData)).Info(\"Audit event\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n",

identity: The numeric identity of the subject\n// - policy: A string identifier for the policy being evaluated\n// - verdict: The decision result (e.g., \"allow\", \"deny\")\n// - reason: A string explaining the decision\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n// - ctx: Context for the operation\n// - policyKey: The policy types.Key being evaluated\n// - selectorCache: The SelectorCache used for identity matching\n// - result: A boolean indicating if the policy evaluation allowed or denied\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey types.Key, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tresultStr := \"deny\"\n\tif result {\n\t\tresultStr = \"allow\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Create structured log entry with audit information\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"policyKey\":      policyKey.String(),\n\t\t\"evaluationResult\": resultStr,\n\t}\n\n\t// Include selector cache information if available\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\t// Add cache size information for audit trail\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RLock()\n\t\tcacheSize := len(selectorCache.idCache)\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tfields[\"selectorCacheSize\"] = cacheSize\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(fields).Info(\"Policy evaluation\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.log = auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level of the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n\n// LogAuditJSON logs structured audit information as JSON for programmatic parsing.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogAuditJSON(auditData map[string]interface{}) error {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Convert to JSON string for logging\n\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(auditData)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpal.log.WithError(err).Error(\"Failed to marshal audit data to JSON\")\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithField(\"audit_json\", string(jsonData)).Info(\"Audit event\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n",

identity: The numeric identity of the subject\n// - policy: A string identifier for the policy being evaluated\n// - verdict: The decision result (e.g., \"allow\", \"deny\")\n// - reason: A string explaining the decision\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.\n//\n// Parameters:\n// - ctx: Context for the operation\n// - policyKey: The policy types.Key being evaluated\n// - selectorCache: The SelectorCache used for identity matching\n// - result: A boolean indicating if the policy evaluation allowed or denied\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey types.Key, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result bool) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tresultStr := \"deny\"\n\tif result {\n\t\tresultStr = \"allow\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Create structured log entry with audit information\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"policyKey\":      policyKey.String(),\n\t\t\"evaluationResult\": resultStr,\n\t}\n\n\t// Include selector cache information if available\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\t// Add cache size information for audit trail\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RLock()\n\t\tcacheSize := len(selectorCache.idCache)\n\t\tselectorCache.mutex.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tfields[\"selectorCacheSize\"] = cacheSize\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithFields(fields).Info(\"Policy evaluation\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.log = auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level of the PolicyAuditLogger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n\n// LogAuditJSON logs structured audit information as JSON for programmatic parsing.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogAuditJSON(auditData map[string]interface{}) error {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Convert to JSON string for logging\n\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(auditData)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpal.log.WithError(err).Error(\"Failed to marshal audit data to JSON\")\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tpal.log.WithField(\"audit_json\", string(jsonData)).Info(\"Audit event\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n",

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types"
)

var auditLog = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, "policy-audit")

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
	lock.Mutex
	logLevel logrus.Level
	log      *logrus.Entry
}

// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level.
func NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {
	return &PolicyAuditLogger{
		logLevel: level,
		log:      auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level),
	}
}

// LogDecision logs a policy decision with structured fields.
//
// Parameters:
// - identity: The numeric identity of the subject
// - policy: A string identifier for the policy being evaluated
// - verdict: The decision result (e.g., "allow", "deny")
// - reason: A string explaining the decision
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict string, reason string) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	pal.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Identity: identity,
		"policy":           policy,
		"verdict":          verdict,
		"reason":           reason,
	}).Info("Policy decision")
}

// LogEvaluation logs the result of a policy evaluation.
//
// Parameters:
// - ctx: Context for the operation
// - policyKey: The policy types.Key being evaluated
// - selectorCache: The SelectorCache used for identity matching
// - 
... (truncated)

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"testing"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/trafficdirection"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types"
)

func TestNewPolicyAuditLogger(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)
	assert.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.GetLogLevel())
}

func TestLogDecision(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)

	// Test logging a decision
	testID := identity.NumericIdentity(1234)
	policy := "test-policy"
	verdict := "allow"
	reason := "matches selector"

	// This should not panic and should complete successfully
	logger.LogDecision(testID, policy, verdict, reason)

	// Verify the logger is still functional
	assert.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.GetLogLevel())
}

func TestLogDecisionDeny(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)

	// Test logging a deny decision
	testID := identity.NumericIdentity(5678)
	policy := "deny-policy"
	verdict := "deny"
	reason := "no matching rule"

	logger.LogDecision(testID, policy, verdict, reason)

	// Verify the logger is still functional
	assert.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.GetLogLevel())
}

func TestLogEvaluation(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)

4. EDIT /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go

// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	pal.logLevel = level
	pal.log = auditLog.Logger.WithLevel(level)
}
After
// SetLogLevel updates the log level for the PolicyAuditLogger.
// Note: This configures the desired log level for the logger. The actual
// output is controlled by the underlying logrus logger configuration.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	pal.logLevel = level
}

import re

def verify_implementation():
    with open('pkg/policy/audit_logger.go', 'r') as f:
        impl = f.read()
    
    with open('pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go', 'r') as f:
        tests = f.read()
    
    print("=== Implementation Verification ===\n")
    
    # Check struct definition
    struct_match = re.search(r'type PolicyAuditLogger struct \{([^}]*)\}', impl, re.DOTALL)
    if struct_match:
        fields = struct_match.group(1)
        required_fields = ['Mutex', 'logLevel', 'log']
        print("✓ PolicyAuditLogger struct found with fields:")
        for field in ['Mutex', 'logLevel', 'log']:
            if field in fields or field.lower() in fields:
                print(f"  ✓ {field}")
            else:
                print(f"  ✗ {field}")
    
    # Check methods
    print("\n✓ Methods found:")
    methods = ['NewPolicyAuditLogger', 'LogDecision', 'LogEvaluation', 'SetLogLevel', 'GetLogLevel', 'LogAuditJSON']
    for method in methods:
        if f'func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) {method}' in impl or f'func {method}' in impl:
            print(f"  ✓ {method}")
        else:
            print(f"  ✗ {method}")
    
    # Check imports
    print("\n✓ Required imports:")
    imports = [
        'logrus',
        'identity',
        'lock',
        'logging',
        'logfields',
        'types',
    ]
    for imp in imports:
        if imp in impl:
            print(f"  ✓ {imp}")
        else:
            print(f"  ✗ {imp}")
    
    # Check thread safety
    print("\n✓ Thread safety:")
    if 'lock.Mutex' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Uses lock.Mutex")
    if 'pal.Lock()' in impl and 'pal.Unlock()' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Methods use Lock/Unlock")
    if 'defer pal.Unlock()' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Uses defer for unlock")
    
    # Check logging
    print("\n✓ Logging framework:")
    if 'logrus.Fields' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Uses logrus.Fields for structured logging")
    if 'logfields.LogSubsys' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Uses logfields constants")
    if '.WithFields' in impl:
        print("  ✓ Uses WithFields for structured data")
    
    # Check test coverage
    print("\n✓ Test coverage:")
    test_funcs = re.findall(r'func (Test\w+)\(', tests)
    print(f"  ✓ {len(test_funcs)} test functions")
    critical_tests = ['TestNewPolicyAuditLogger', 'TestLogDecision', 'TestLogEvaluation', 'TestSetLogLevel']
    for test in critical_tests:
        if test in test_funcs:
            print(f"    ✓ {test}")
        else:
            print(f"    ✗ {test}")
    
    # Check test imports
    print("\n✓ Test imports:")
    test_imports = ['testing', 'logrus', 'require', 'assert', 'identity', 'types']
    for imp in test_imports:
        if imp in tests:
            print(f"  ✓ {imp}")
    
    print("\n=== Verification Complete ===")

verify_implementation()
